### Round 6: Monaco Grand Prix
*Date: 2008-05-25*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 11: Hungarian Grand Prix
*Date: 2008-08-03*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 16: Japanese Grand Prix
*Date: 2008-10-12*

#### Qualifying Results
